\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!frexp@{frexp}}
\index{frexp@{frexp}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{frexp()}{frexp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaddf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}{glm::\+frexp}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{int \&}]{exp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Splits x into a floating-\/point significand in the range \+[0.\+5, 1.\+0) and an integral exponent of two, such that:\+ x = significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

The significand is returned by the function and the exponent is returned in the parameter exp. For a floating-\/point value of zero, the significant and exponent are both zero. For a floating-\/point value that is an infinity or is not a number, the results are undefined.

\end{DoxyTemplParams}

To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.

\index{intBitsToFloat@{intBitsToFloat}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intBitsToFloat()}{intBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128}{glm::\+int\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a signed integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Builds a floating-\/point number from x and the corresponding integral exponent of two in exp, returning:\+ significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

If this product is too large to be represented in the floating-\/point type, the result is undefined.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!mix@{mix}}
\index{mix@{mix}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mix()}{mix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416} 
template$<$typename gen\+TypeT, typename gen\+TypeU$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a08b807947b47031d3a511f03f89645ad}{GLM\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR}} gen\+TypeT \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416}{glm::\+mix}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{y}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeU}]{a}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If gen\+TypeU is a floating scalar or vector:\+ Returns x \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (1.\+0 -\/ a) + y \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} a, i.\+e., the linear blend of x and y using the floating-\/point value a. The value for a is not restricted to the range \+[0, 1]\+.

If gen\+TypeU is a boolean scalar or vector:\+ Selects which vector each returned component comes from. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is false, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} is returned. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is true, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} is returned. Components of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} that are not selected are allowed to be invalid floating point values and will have no effect on the results. Thus, this provides different functionality than gen\+Type mix(gen\+Type x, gen\+Type y, gen\+Type(a)) where a is a Boolean vector.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/mix.xml}{\texttt{GLSL mix man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{glad_8h_a92d0386e5c19fb81ea88c9f99644ab1d}{x}} & Value to interpolate. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{glad_8h_a66ddd433d2cacfe27f5906b7e86faeed}{y}} & Value to interpolate. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{glad_8h_ac8729153468b5dcf13f971b21d84d4e5}{a}} & Interpolant.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+TypeT} & Floating point scalar or vector. \\
\hline
{\em gen\+TypeU} & Floating point or boolean scalar or vector. It can\textquotesingle{}t be a vector if it is the length of gen\+TypeT.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\doxymbox{\hyperlink{glm_8hpp}{glm/glm.hpp}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{...}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a85e33f139b8db1b39b590a5713b9e679} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga85e33f139b8db1b39b590a5713b9e679}{glm::\+modf}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+Type \&}]{i}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the fractional part of x and sets i to the integer part (as a whole number floating point value). Both the return value and the output parameter will have the same sign as x.

Creates a matrix for projecting two-\/dimensional coordinates onto the screen.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a8dd6ed0963b92e610448163d12f20dc7}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!orthoLH@{orthoLH}}
\index{orthoLH@{orthoLH}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{orthoLH()}{orthoLH()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a8dd6ed0963b92e610448163d12f20dc7} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga8dd6ed0963b92e610448163d12f20dc7}{glm::\+ortho\+LH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{left}{, }\item[{T}]{right}{, }\item[{T}]{bottom}{, }\item[{T}]{top}{, }\item[{T}]{z\+Near}{, }\item[{T}]{z\+Far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for an orthographic parallel viewing volume, using left-\/handed coordinates. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)

\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!perspective@{perspective}}
\index{perspective@{perspective}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perspective()}{perspective()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}{glm::\+perspective}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a symmetric perspective-\/view frustum based on the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\href{https://www.khronos.org/registry/OpenGL-Refpages/gl2.1/xhtml/gluPerspective.xml}{\texttt{glu\+Perspective man page}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\

Creates a matrix for a left-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a703204a33716e0eefc1a6ff383ab62ed} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga703204a33716e0eefc1a6ff383ab62ed}{glm::\+perspective\+RH\+\_\+\+ZO}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a right-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. The near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\

Creates a matrix for a symmetric perspective-\/view frustum using left-\/handed coordinates if GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED if defined or right-\/handed coordinates otherwise. The near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest. This includes the possibility that round(x) returns the same value as round\+Even(x) for all values of x.

Spherical linear interpolation of two quaternions. The interpolation always take the short path and the rotation is performed at constant speed.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!smoothstep@{smoothstep}}
\index{smoothstep@{smoothstep}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{smoothstep()}{smoothstep()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}{glm::\+smoothstep}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge0}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge1}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns 0.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= edge0 and 1.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1 and performs smooth Hermite interpolation between 0 and 1 when edge0 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} edge1. This is useful in cases where you would want a threshold function with a smooth transition. This is equivalent to:\+ gen\+Type t; t = clamp ((x -\/ edge0) /\+ (edge1 -\/ edge0), 0, 1); return t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (3 -\/ 2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t); Results are undefined if edge0 \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & Floating-\/point scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/smoothstep.xml}{\texttt{GLSL smoothstep man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!uintBitsToFloat@{uintBitsToFloat}}
\index{uintBitsToFloat@{uintBitsToFloat}!glm::ext@{glm::ext}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uintBitsToFloat()}{uintBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac}{glm::\+uint\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a unsigned integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/uintBitsToFloat.xml}{\texttt{GLSL uint\+Bits\+To\+Float man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unProject()}{unProject()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_aefa35b1dbf52941052a5a3aadc298106} 
template$<$typename T, typename U, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__projection_gaefa35b1dbf52941052a5a3aadc298106}{glm::\+un\+Project}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{win}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{model}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{proj}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 4, U, Q $>$ const \&}]{viewport}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Map the specified window coordinates (win.\+x, win.\+y, win.\+z) into object coordinates using default near and far clip planes definition. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em win} & Specify the window coordinates to be mapped. \\
\hline
{\em model} & Specifies the modelview matrix \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__gtx__projection_ga58384b7170801dd513de46f87c7fb00e}{proj}} & Specifies the projection matrix \\
\hline
{\em viewport} & Specifies the viewport \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the computed object coordinates. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & Native type used for the computation. Currently supported:\+ half (not recommended), float or double. \\
\hline
{\em U} & Currently supported:\+ Floating-\/point types and integer types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a9d915647ec33c4110946665f914d3abb}\index{glm::ext@{glm::ext}!uround@{uround}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uround()}{uround()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1ext_a9d915647ec33c4110946665f914d3abb} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__common_ga9d915647ec33c4110946665f914d3abb}{glm::\+uround}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type const \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
